A routed bathhouse controller: the page turns the drawing into executable plumbing — label the channels, then cycle/settle across nodes until the whole network converges.

## Multilens Translation Atlas

### AQM

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\rho_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}}(\rho_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-), \qquad \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} = \mathsf O_{\texttt{laly}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{alkedy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{dylches}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{qopchedy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{qopchedy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{chey}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{qokol}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{p!!!aldarairal}}\]

  Variable legend: `rho^-` incoming folio line state; `rho^+` outgoing line state; `Phi_line^(AQM)` source operator chain.
  Reading: root fixation / circulation command / fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P.10`
  Equation:

### Hacking Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_1}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_1}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_1}}\]

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: root fixation / circulation command / fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

A routed bathhouse controller: the page turns the drawing into executable plumbing — label the channels, then cycle/settle across nodes until the whole network converges. Process statistics: 111 circulation commands (qo-); 6 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 16 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 11 completion markers (daiin); 2 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f77r` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=54, N_valve=8, and N_seal=2. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f77r` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`A routed bathhouse controller: the page turns the drawing into executable plumbing — label the channels, then cycle/settle across nodes until the whole network converges.`

## Dense One-Sentence Compression

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f77r} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
